	GNG_PTRG_deadline = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Malaya
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Indonesia
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Colombia
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_OC
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 365
		allowed = {
			tag = GNG
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Malaya
				}
				clr_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Select_GUI_3_choices_Visible
				GNG_PTRG_Malaya_END = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Indonesia
				}
				clr_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Select_GUI_2_choices_Visible
				GNG_PTRG_Indonesia_END = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Colombia
				}
				clr_country_flag = GNG_PTRG_Select_GUI_1_choices_Visible
				GNG_PTRG_Colombia_END = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {

				}

		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		allowed = {
			tag = GNG
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = GNG.kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = modifier@GNG_kenpeitai_growth_modifier }
				GNG_kenpeitai_control_change = yes
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = GNG.kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var }
				add_to_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = modifier@GNG_kenpeitai_growth_modifier }
				GNG_kenpeitai_control_change = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GNG_enable_harder_underworld }
				custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_because_expanded_underworld_tt
				random_owned_state = {
					set_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = GNG.kenpeitai_growth_quarterly_var }
					add_to_temp_variable = { ken_spt_temp = modifier@GNG_kenpeitai_growth_modifier }

				}
			}

			}
		}

GNG_Riots_GUI = {
	GNG_negotiations_30days_stall_deadline_GFT = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		priority = 1000
		days_mission_timeout = 30
		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_negotiations_30days_stall_deadline_GFT_CCL_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { strength = GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength }
				set_temp_variable = { radicalism = GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism }
				set_temp_variable = { aver = strength }
				add_to_temp_variable = { aver = radicalism }
				divide_temp_variable = { aver = 2 }
				set_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value = aver }
				divide_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value = 10 }
				add_to_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value = 0.5 } #Ensures demands always round up
				round_variable = GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value
				multiply_variable = { GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value = 10 }

				log = "GNG PROPOSALS NEGOTIATIONS: GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value == [?GNG_Proposals_Counter_Value]"

				country_event = guangdong_RiotsNegotiations.7
			}
		}
	}

	GNG_speak_to_the_japanese_consul_general = {

				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_takashima_special_chances > 2.5 } }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general < 6 } }
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.200
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general = 6 } }
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.203
					}
					else = {
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.202
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { GNG_takashima_special_chances > 1.5 } }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general < 5 } }
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.200
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general = 5 } }
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.203
					}
					else = {
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.202
					}
				}
				else_if = {

						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.200
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general = 4 } }
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.203
					}
					else = {
						country_event = guangdong_commonRiots.202
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { GNG_speak_to_the_consul_general < 3 } }

					}

	#Mission timeout ticks to let player know of the next tick
	GNG_the_situation_updates = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GNG_disable_all_mechanics_IJA }
			has_country_flag = GNG_Riots_Active
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = GNG_IJA_Intervenes
			}
		}
		activation = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no

		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 14 # 15 days to timeout

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: GNG_the_situation_worsens mission timer elapsed"
			randomize_variable = {
				var = riot_growth_next
				distribution = uniform
				min = 1
				max = 4.49 #Oddly specific value is to make sure that 3.5 and 4 are more normal values
			}
			round_variable = riot_growth_next
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { riot_growth_next > 1 } } #This is to generate x.5 or x.0 values
					random_list = {
						1 = {

						}
						1 = {
							subtract_from_variable = { riot_growth_next = 0.5 }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
						has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
					}
				}

				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_commonRiots.9
						hours = 3
					}
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_IJA_InterventionPossible
						check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots > 30 }
						check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots < 50 }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
					}
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
					add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
					}
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
					add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots_Temp = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick }
				random_owned_state = {
					set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = GNG.riot_growth_next }
					GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = GNG.riot_growth_next }
					GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
				}
				GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
				GNG_Despair_Change = yes
				GNG_Japanese_Intervention_Change = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GNG_the_situation_updates
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_IJARiots.1
						hours = 3
					}
				}
			}

			else_if = {
				limit = {

						has_country_flag = GNG_IJA_InterventionPossible

					add_to_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Temp = GNG_Riots_Strength_Tick }
					set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Temp = GNG_Riots_Radicalism_Tick }
				}
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_Riots_Despair_Temp = GNG_Riots_Despair_Tick }
				set_temp_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots_Temp = GNG_Riots_Japanese_Intervention_Tick }
				random_owned_state = {
					set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = GNG.riot_growth_next }
					GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
				}
				random_owned_state = {
					set_temp_variable = { riot_spt_temp = GNG.riot_growth_next }
					GNG_rioters_control_change = yes
				}
				GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_GFT_Radicalism_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_CCL_Strength_Change = yes
				GNG_Riots_CCL_Radicalism_Change = yes
				GNG_Despair_Change = yes
				GNG_Japanese_Intervention_Change = yes
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = GNG_the_situation_updates
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				random_list = {
					1 = {

					}
					2 = {
						GNG_fire_riots_event = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick = {#Mission timeout ticks to let player know next strength check
		icon = GFX_decision_GNG_GFT
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GNG_disable_all_mechanics_IJA }
			has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_Happening
		}
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_Happening
		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 14 # 15 days to timeout

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick mission timer elapsed"
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_Riots_GFT_Strength < 30 }
					}
					activate_mission = GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick
				}
				else = {
					remove_mission = GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission GNG_GFT_dismantlement_tick Completed"
		}
	}

			}

			has_country_flag = GNG_IJAInterventionImminent
		}

		}

		fire_only_once = no
		days_mission_timeout = 9 #10 days to timeout

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: GNG_Japan_Intervenes mission timer elapsed"
			custom_effect_tooltip = GNG_Japan_Intervenes_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots < 95 }
					}
					clr_country_flag = GNG_IJAInterventionImminent
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_IJARiots.20
						hours = 3
					}
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_GFT_OVER
							has_country_flag = GNG_Dismantlement_CCL_OVER
						}
					}
					clr_country_flag = GNG_IJAInterventionImminent
					clr_country_flag = GNG_IJA_InterventionPossible
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_IJARiots.21
						hours = 3
					}
				}

				else_if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { GNG_Japan_Riots > 95 }
						}
					}
					clr_country_flag = GNG_IJAInterventionImminent
					set_country_flag = GNG_IJA_Intervenes
					country_event = {
						id = guangdong_IJARiots.6
						hours = 3
					}
					remove_mission = GNG_the_situation_updates
				}
			}
		}
